  <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function(){
      $("ul.subnav").parent().append("<span></span>"); //Only shows drop down trigger when js is enabled - Adds empty span tag after ul.subnav
      $("ul.topnav li a") .mouseover(function() { //When trigger is clicked...
        //Following events are applied to the subnav itself (moving subnav up and down)
        $(this).parent().find("ul.subnav").slideDown('fast').show();
        //Drop down the subnav on click
        $(this).parent().hover(function() {
        }, function(){  
          $(this).parent().find("ul.subnav").slideUp('medium'); //When the mouse hovers out of the subnav, move it back up
        });
        //Following events are applied to the trigger (Hover events for the trigger)
        }).hoverIntent(function() { 
          $(this).addClass("subhover"); //On hover over, add class "subhover"
        }, function(){  //On Hover Out
          $(this).removeClass("subhover"); //On hover out, remove class "subhover"
      });
    });
    </script>

     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <h1 class="page-header">Communications</h1> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <ul class="nav nav-tabs sub-nav tab4"> 
        <li class="active"><a class="" href="index.html">Overview</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="staff/index.html">Staff &amp; Contacts</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="what-we-do/index.html">What we do</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="resources/index.html">Resources</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- Example row of columns --> 
     <div class="row-fluid"> 
      <div class="span4 hero-unit"> 
       <p>We tell the UC story with clarity and conviction.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4">
       <p>Communications builds public awareness of UC’s value and its impact on the lives of people in California and beyond. Working with campus colleagues, OP leaders and our clients, we respond to critical issues; convey the breadth and depth of UC’s leadership in teaching, research and public service; and foster pride and engagement in the UC community.</p>
      </div> 
      <div class="span4"> 
       <div class="row-fluid dotted-bottom"> 
        <div class="span8"> 
         <p class="blue"> Peter King and Katherine Edwards </p> 
         <p>Executive Directors</p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row-fluid"> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon staff" href="staff/index.html">Staff Directory</a>
        </div> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon org" href="_files/comm_org_chart.pdf">Org Chart</a>
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span4 blustripe"> 
       <h2 class="allCaps"> What we do </h2> 
       <ul class="dotted-list"> 
        <li> <a href="what-we-do/marketing-communications.html">Marketing communications</a> </li> 
        <li> <a href="what-we-do/public-affairs.html">Public affairs &amp; media relations</a> </li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4 blustripe"> 
       <h2 class="allCaps"> Work with us </h2> 
       <ul class="dotted-list"> 
        <li> <a href="what-we-do/before-you-call.html">Before you call</a> </li>

     <img src="/Images/holds.png" alt="" class="page-lead" /> 
     <div class="span-11"> 
      <h3>Clear Holds on Your Account </h3> 
      <p> Clear any holds on your account before your registration appointment so that you can register on time. Administrative offices place holds on your account <strong>when you fail to: </strong></p> 
      <ul class="orange-bullets"> 
       <li>Comply with admission requirements</li> 
       <li>Settle financial obligations with the university</li> 
       <li>Respond to official notices</li> 
       <li>Submit requested documents</li> 
       <li>Complete the required hepatitis B vaccination </li> 
      </ul> 
      <p> If you have a hold on your account, you may not be able to register for classes, receive financial aid, use campus services, or obtain your transcripts or diploma. </p> 
      <p>Please click on the Holds section within Growl to view any holds you may have, their description and who to contact to resolve the hold.</p> 
      <p> In most cases, the office that placed the hold is the only one that can release it. If you have questions, we recommend contacting that office directly.</p> 
     </div>

  <div class="pagewrapper"> 
   <h3 class="accessibility">Footer</h3> 
   <div id="colophon">
     The University of California, Riverside (
    <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/">www.ucr.edu</a>) is a doctoral research university, a living laboratory for groundbreaking exploration of issues critical to Inland Southern California, the state and communities around the world. Reflecting California's diverse culture, UCR's enrollment has exceeded 21,000 students. The campus opened a medical school in 2013 and has reached the heart of the Coachella Valley by way of the UCR Palm Desert Center. The campus has an annual statewide economic impact of more than $1 billion. A broadcast studio with fiber cable to the AT&amp;T Hollywood hub is available for live or taped interviews. UCR also has ISDN for radio interviews. To learn more, call (951) UCR-NEWS. 
   </div>
